  1. You might think I'm insane if you're reading the other reviews for this product. I don't mean to imply that these strips won't cause sensitivity and pain. They do. But the thing is, if you have really sensitive teeth and gums, EVERY whitening product causes serious pain for several days after use. I finally realized this. In the past, I tried using the normal white strips only every 3-4 days, but I still had to suffer every single time I used them. The so called &#34;gentle&#34; white strips are the same. So I'd keep buying these boxes desperately wanting to whiten my teeth, but it was torturous and I never used more than maybe 8 or so and then the rest would end up never used. So I changed strategies. When I bought the express white strips, I also bought the new Crest Sensi-Stop Strips (warning, the Sensi-Stop strips are ridiculously tiny, and I used the whole six pack in one go to cover the area the white strips covered, but the protection lasts for a month so it worked out). I used the one hour express whitening strips for 2 hours, then I immediately applied the Sensi-Stop strips. I am happy to report that the usual excruciating pain I have in the days after using teeth whitening strips is significantly reduced using this strategy! Now, one set of the one hour express strips only whitens a few shades. I am going to go ahead and used the other 3 sets of whitening strips this week and while I don't expect crazy white teeth, I can already tell the results of this experiment will be much better than my previous (very painful) experiences. If you have ridiculous sensitivity issues, this is a much less painful, drawn-out way to get nice pearly whites. I'm not promising you will have zero pain, but if you're like me, even half as much pain would be much more tolerable. This method definitely achieved that.

  30. I've been a user of the original 14-day Crest White Strips for years, and have always been happy with the results. My teeth aren't terribly stained, but I do drink coffee and wine regularly and like to brighten them up from time to time. The strips are just as easy to use as the original, and in fact are much \\"stickier\\" - there is a lot less slipping than with the 2-week kind. Keeping them in for two hours turned out to be a lot less comfortable that the 30 minutes needed for the 14-day version - my teeth started to ache a bit (and I don't have sensitive teeth), plus it is hard to completely relax your mouth while you are aware of these strips, so my jaw was a little achy towards the end. They are harder to remove than the original (because of the increased stickiness) - but that's not big deal. However, after removing them and cleaning the residual goo off of my teeth, I was disappointed. They were whiter, but not nearly as white as at the end of the 14-day treatment. The instructions say the results should last 3 months, but don't clearly indicate whether it is safe to use them more frequently, so I don't know if I can try another application sooner to see if I can improve the results (there are 4 sets of strips in the box).<br /><br />2 hours was a long time to keep them in, and that 2 hours included discomfort I don't feel with the 14-day version. I think I'll go back to the 14-day version - popping them on after breakfast in the morning for 30 minutes (more than the time it takes me to shower, get dressed and get ready to leave the house) is much easier and the results are much more noticeable. Besides, as a random fringe benefit, I've noticed that the \\"oh so clean\\" feeling you have after using the strips discourages snacking for a while, so 2 weeks of no mid-morning munchies (or do them at night if that's your weak time) leaves you smiling brighter AND maybe a bit skinnier!'s your weak time) leaves you smiling brighter AND maybe a bit skinnier!

I thought that they would help with maintaining the whiteness in between periodic visits to the dentist for teeth check-ups and cleaning. The original Crest Whitestrips easily moved around or slid off my teeth, sometimes within minutes after I put them on my teeth.<br /><br />I then used three boxes of the [[ASIN:B00336EUTK Crest 3D White Whitestrips With Advanced Seal Professional Effects Enamel Safe Dental Whitening Kit, 20-count Carton]] when that product became available. The 20-strip box of that version is designed to be worn for 30 minutes, once a day. Compared to the original Crest Whitestrips, the \\"Advanced Seal\\" technology really does work to hold the strips firmly to the teeth. On my teeth, the lower strip sometimes does not stick as well as the upper strip, which always sticks as firmly as duct tape.<br /><br />The instructions recommend that you do not brush your teeth before application. But I brushed my teeth anyway whenever I applied the strips after eating a meal. Once I used my fingers to firmly press the strip onto my upper and lower teeth, the strips never moved around the way the original Whitestrips did. But even though the advertisements say that you can talk and drink water while wearing the strips, I always avoided drinking water while wearing the strips out of concern that too much fluid may dilute the peroxide whitening agent. After all, these products are not exactly inexpensive, and I want to get my money's worth of whitening with each application! :-) I also doubt that you can, or would want to, eat while wearing the \\"Advanced Seal\\" strips. Although it is far easier to talk while wearing the \\"Advanced Seal\\" strips compared with the original Whitestrips (which could easily be moved or dislodged with the slightest mouth movements), with the \\"Advanced Seal\\" strips stuck to my teeth, my speech was usually slightly altered, as if I had a bit of peanut butter in my mouth or as if I was wearing braces. But other than not drinking/eating and minimizing my talking, I could go about my daily routines while wearing them. The instructions say not to use these strips on loose teeth because the \\"Advanced Seal\\" truly feels like duct tape firmly stuck to your teeth. You would not want to use these strips' strong adhesion on any loose teeth. When you peel the strips off, there is a slightly odd aftertaste, but it was not disagreeable to me and can be easily washed away by rinsing with water.<br /><br />Which brings me to this newest addition to the Crest Whitestrip product line... The advertisement for this new Whitestrip is certainly enticing - all you have to do is get this box of 4 pairs of Whitestrips, and wear a strip for just 2 hours, repeating the treatment 3 months later, for a full year's worth of whitening. During my testing of this new Whitestrip, instead of waiting 3 months before using another application, I waited 2 weeks later and then applied another Whitestrip. Compared to the [[ASIN:B00336EUTK Crest 3D White Whitestrips With Advanced Seal Professional Effects Enamel Safe Dental Whitening Kit, 20-count Carton]], these new strips have two notches in the upper/lower strips that help the strips to tuck behind your teeth edge more easily. The adhesive on these new Whitestrips seem to be a bit stickier than before even though the previous \\"Professional Effects\\" Advanced Seal was already quite sticky.<br /><br />The verdict after two applications within a two week period? I do see some incremental whitening. However, I really wonder how well this whitening will last during the 3-month period before I use another one of these \\"Express\\" strips again.   123. The Crest 2 Hour Express Whitestrips and 3D White Rinse is one of Crest's many products in their at-home teeth-whitening line. It differentiates itself from their other products, by promising noticeable whiter teeth in just two hours, with results expected to last up to three months. The box contains four treatments, so it may be more economical than their other products, since the price per treatment is not as expensive (most other Crest products require you to use the entire box for a treatment).<br /><br />Once you get the hang of it, putting the strips on is fairly easy. It is a clear piece of plastic with a layer of hydrogen peroxide covering the strip. Two strips (for top and bottom teeth) come in a treatment, and lay over the teeth so that the peroxide presses down onto them and coats them. Although you can talk pretty easily with the strips on, I've found that the more you move your mouth around, the easier it is for the strips to slide around and move out of place. So I advise not to talk during the treatment. The treatment lasts two hours, which is much longer than the usual 30 minutes their other treatments take. Although the strips are not uncomfortable, it was kind of a pain to keep them in my mouth this long, so I was thankful I only had to do it once.<br /><br />After removing the strips, I rinsed my mouth out with water and checked the results. I did not notice any real difference in my teeth (I left the bottom teeth completely uncovered so I could compare). They did appear whiter, but only very slightly, and not enough to justify the product's use. What I did notice was a very painful sensation in my teeth from the peroxide. I am very familiar with the Crest strips, and I take precautions, such as using [[ASIN:B001OOLF82 Sensodyne Pronamel Gentle Whitening Toothpaste, Alpine Breeze, 4-Ounce Tubes (Pack of 3)]] toothpaste for weeks prior to application, and weeks afterwords. Even still, my teeth hurt a lot, and I had a sensation that you would expect from chewing aluminum foil with your teeth. It was very unpleasant. I don't know if this is caused by the hydrogen peroxide concentration, or from the longer application time, but I won't be trying the strips out again. I believe it was probably due to the longer application time, since I've used [[ASIN:B000XS3FYM Crest Whitestrips Supreme Professional Strength 84 strips]] many times in the past (higher concentration of hydrogen peroxide than normal strips) and been able to handle it. Additionally, the whitening I did obtain, did not last anywhere near three months, and faded after about three weeks.<br /><br />While I do think Crest makes a very good product with their whitestrips line, I don't think the 2-Hr Express whitening strips are a good complement to it. For anyone who wants whiter teeth, I suggest they try the [[ASIN:B000XS3FYM Crest Whitestrips Supreme Professional Strength 84 strips]] or the [[ASIN:B00336EUTK Crest 3D White Whitestrips With Advanced Seal Professional Effects Enamel Safe Dental Whitening Kit, 20-count Carton]], and make sure to use Sensodyne during the treatment. Additionally, don't ever leave the strips on longer than the directions states. It won't make your teeth any whiter, just more painful.rom chewing aluminum foil with your teeth. It was very unpleasant. I don't know if this is caused by the hydrogen peroxide concentration, or from the longer application time, but I won't be trying the strips out again.
